 The water level in the Bhakra Dam has reached an all-time high, following which the Bhakra Beas Management Board (BBMB) today issued a warning to the Punjab government that it would release excess water into the Sutlej and Beas rivers in the next few days
 board ke adhyaksh abi agarwal ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, is sijan main hamaare jalaashyon (bhakhda or beas) main jalastr lagaataar bad rahaa he
 (in Bhakra) Water level is highest in last 40-50 years
 unhone kaha, hamane bhakhda kii sthiti se punjab ke mukhyamantri prakaash singh badal ko avgat karaane ke liye 5 july ko unke saath baithak kii thi
 Aggarwal said that due to heavy snow melt and pre-monsoon rains, the water level is increasing and additional water needs to be released in the next few days
 unhone kaha, main logon ko aashwaasan dena chahta hum ki ham niyantrit tareeke se pani chodenge taaki baadh nahin aae, lekin chetavanee ke taur par kaha ja rahaa he ki yadi uttarakhand jaisi sthiti hogi to bibiembi yaa duniya kaa koi bhi anya sanghathan asahaay hoga
 Aggarwal said that the water level in Bhakra will cross the 1645 feet level in the next 7-8 days
 jab unase poocha gaya ki kitna pani choda jayega to unhone kaha ki yah is baat par nirbhar karegaa ki us vakt pani kaa bahaav kaisaa he
 He said, due to heavy rains and maximum melting of snow this year, it seems that the water level will reach the set level well in advance
 pani chode jane kii puri sambhaavna he, kyonki abhi puraa monsoon sijan padaa he
 Bhakra and Pong dams are to be filled up to 1680 and 1390 feet respectively by September this year
 unhone kaha ki pichley kai varshon main bhakhda baandh main baadh kii sambhaavna kai guna bad gai he
 Blaming the illegal construction around the Sutlej and Beas rivers for this, he said, if you go through the districts of Beas and Sutlej (of Punjab), you will find encroachment
 aapako koi aisa sthaan nahin milegaa jahaan atikaraman nahin hua he
 He put the responsibility of stopping the encroachment on the Punjab government
 badal ne kal ropar, navanshahar, ferozepur, jalandhar, hoshiyarpur, moga or kapoothrala ke upayuktaon ko kisi bhi aakasmik sthiti se nibatane ke liye paryaapt intjaam karne kaa nirdesh diya tha
 The comments chetavanee ke maddenjar punjab ke sinchai mantri janameja singh sekhon ne sabhi mukhya abhiyantaaon ko nirdesh diya he ki ve nadiyon or naharon ke tatavarti ilaakon main sabhi samvedansheel sthanon par adhikariyon ko tainaat karen
 Asked by the Bhakra Beas Management Board that illegal construction in the submergence area of sutlej and Beas was responsible for obstructing the free flow of rivers, Sekhon said, "that is not illegal occupation at all
" 
 People own their own land in the river stream and the surrounding area and have built shelter for livestock etc
 However after warning we have asked them to remove their cattle and protect their goods
 mantri ne kaha ki punjab sarkaar pehle hi rajya str ke baadh niyantran kaksh kaa gathan kiya he or vah apatkaal ke dauraan choubison ghante kaam karata rahegaa
 Chairman of the board AB Aggarwal told reporters, the water level in our reservoirs (bhakra and Beas) is continuously increasing this season
 (bhakhda main) jalastr pichley 40-50 saalon main sarvaadhik he
 He said, We had a meeting with him on July 5 to apprise Punjab Chief Minister Parkash Singh Badal about the situation in Bhakra
 agarwal ne kaha ki baari maatra main barf ke pighalane evam monsoon purv barish ke chalate jalastr badhata ja rahaa he or agle kuch dinon main atirikt pani chode jane kii jarurat he
 "I want to assure the people that we will release water in a controlled manner so that there will not be floods, but it is being said that if there is a situation like Uttarakhand, then BBMB or any other organization of the world will be helpless
" agarwal ne kaha ki bhakhda main jalastr agle 7-8 dinon main 1645 foot ke str ko paar kar jayega
 When asked how much water would be released, he said that it would depend on how the water flow at that time
 unhone kaha, is saal baari barish evam barf ke adhiktam pighalane ke kaaran lagata he ki pani kaa str kaaphi pehle hi nirdhaarit str tak pahunch jayega
 There is every possibility of release of water, as the entire monsoon season has just passed
 bhakhda or pong baandh is saal sitambar tak kramash: 1680 or 1390 feet tak bhare jane hai
 He said that the probability of flooding in Bhakra Dam has increased manifold in the last several years
 iske liye sutluj or beas nadiyon ke aasapaas avaidh nirmaan ko jimmedaar tehraate hue kaha, beas or sutluj (punjab ke) jin jilon se guzarati hai, yadi aap vahaan jaaen to aap atikaraman paaenge
 You will not find any place where there is no encroachment
 atikaraman rokane kii jimmedaari unhone punjab sarkaar par daal di
 Badal yesterday directed the Deputy Commissioners of Ropar, Nawanshahar, Ferozepur, Jalandhar, Hoshiarpur, Moga and Kaputharla to make adequate arrangements to deal with any unforeseen situation
 tippaniyan In view of the warning, Punjab Irrigation Minister Janmeja Singh Sekhon has directed all the Chief Engineers to deploy officers at all sensitive places along the rivers and canals
 bhakhda beas prabandhan board kii ore se sutluj or beas ke dub kshetra main avaidh nirmaan ko nadiyon ke mukt bahaav main baadha ke liye jimmedaar bataae jane par sekhon ne kaha, vah avaidh kabja bilkul nahin he
 
 nadiyon kii dhara or aasapaas ke kshetra main logon kii apni jameen he or unhone pashuon aadi ke liye aashray kaa nirmaan kiya he haalanki chetavanee ke baad hamane unase apane maveshi hataane or apane maal kii suraksha karne ko kaha he
 The minister said that the Punjab government has already set up a state-level flood control room and will continue to work round the clock during the emergency
